<a id="4404" class="Comment">{- Definition 19.1.3. Given a cocone structure on X and a family of maps indexed
   by X, we obtain a morphism of descent data. -}</a>

<a id="12238" class="Comment">{- We construct the identity morphism and composition, and we show that 
   morphisms equipped with two-sided inverses are equivalences. -}</a>

  <a id="15067" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15069" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15069" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="15071" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15073" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#1497" class="Function">hom-Fam-pushout</a> <a id="15089" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15014" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15091" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15039" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="15092" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15094" class="Symbol">→</a>

<a id="15153" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#14889" class="Function">equiv-is-equiv-hom-Fam-pushout</a> <a id="15184" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15184" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15186" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15186" class="Bound">Q</a> <a id="15188" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15188" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="15190" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15190" class="Bound">is-equiv-h</a> <a id="15201" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="15205" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a>
    <a id="15214" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15216" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="15218" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15218" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="15220" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15222" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="15227" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15228" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="15232" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15188" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="15234" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15218" class="Bound">a</a><a id="15235" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15237" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15238" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="15242" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15190" class="Bound">is-equiv-h</a> <a id="15253" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15218" class="Bound">a</a><a id="15254" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="15261" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15263" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a>
      <a id="15274" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15276" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="15278" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15278" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="15280" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15282" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="15287" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15288" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="15292" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15293" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="15297" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15188" class="Bound">h</a><a id="15298" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15300" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15278" class="Bound">b</a><a id="15301" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15303" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15304" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="15308" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15190" class="Bound">is-equiv-h</a> <a id="15319" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15278" class="Bound">b</a><a id="15320" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="15329" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15331" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="15335" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15336" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="15340" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15188" class="Bound">h</a><a id="15341" class="Symbol">)))</a>

<a id="15346" class="Comment">{- Theorem 19.1.3. Characterization of identity types of pushouts. -}</a>

<a id="15417" class="Comment">{-
hom-identity-is-universal-Fam-pushout :
  { l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level} {S : UU l1} {A : UU l2} {B : UU l3} {X : UU l5}
  { f : S → A} {g : S → B} (c : cocone f g X) →
  ( up-X : (l : Level) → universal-property-pushout l f g c) →
  ( P : Fam-pushout l4 f g) (a : A) (p : pr1 P a) →
  is-universal-Fam-pushout l5 P a p →
  Σ ( hom-Fam-pushout P (desc-fam c (Id (pr1 c a))))
    ( λ h → Id (pr1 h a p) refl)
hom-identity-is-universal-Fam-pushout {f = f} {g} c up-X P a p is-univ-P =
  {!!}

is-identity-is-universal-Fam-pushout :
  { l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level} {S : UU l1} {A : UU l2} {B : UU l3} {X : UU l5}
  { f : S → A} {g : S → B} (c : cocone f g X) →
  ( up-X : (l : Level) → universal-property-pushout l f g c) →
  ( P : Fam-pushout l4 f g) (a : A) (p : pr1 P a) →
  is-universal-Fam-pushout l5 P a p →
  Σ ( equiv-Fam-pushout P (desc-fam c (Id (pr1 c a))))
    ( λ e → Id (map-equiv (pr1 e a) p) refl)
is-identity-is-universal-Fam-pushout {f = f} {g} c up-X a P p₀ is-eq-P = {!!}
-}</a>
</pre>
